focus_tree = {
	id = ireland_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = IRE
		}
	}
	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 900 y = 2350 }

	###############################################
	### Black Monday Branch				 		###
	### Design by Zimbabwe Salt Co. & El Daddy  ###

	focus = {
		id = IRE_renovate_rail_line
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_railroad
		cost = 5

		x = -66
		y = 0

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IRE_renovate_rail_line"
			build_railway = {
				level = 1
				path = { 7394 11267 9310 3342 11293 3359 3242 3379 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_tech = basic_train } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_train_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_technology = { basic_train = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = IRE_renovate_rail_line
					bonus = 0.5
					uses = 1
					category = train_tech
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = train_equipment
				amount = 10
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

	focus = {

			if = {
				limit = { date < 1937.2.14 }

					tooltip = IRE_election_over

				}
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IRE_raidio_eireann"
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IRE_raidio_eireann_on_air
				days = 365
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ireland.1500 days = 60 random_days = 30 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war = yes
						has_global_flag = second_weltkrieg_has_started
						controls_state = 119
					}
					country_event = { id = irelandflavour.400 days = 75 random_days = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

	focus = {
		id = IRE_advanced_studies
		icon = GFX_goal_nuclear
		cost = 6

		relative_position_id = IRE_urban_electrification
		x = 0
		y = 1

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = IRE_agrarianism

			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = IRE_urban_electrification }

		ai_will_do = { factor = 1000 }

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IRE_advanced_studies"
			add_research_slot_until_five = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_agrarianism }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_agrarianism_advanced_studies_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_industrialisation }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_industrialisation_advanced_studies_tt
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_apply_one_of_effects_depending_on_ideas
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_agrarianism_advanced_studies_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_industrialisation_advanced_studies_tt
			}
			add_to_variable = { IRE_advanced_studies_research = 0.075 }
			IRE_end_industrialisation_dynmod = yes
			IRE_end_agrarianism_dynmod = yes
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
	}
